\begin{entry}

shiroVBAgavu meVlumxKavAgi, adu modalu AdhAra\-cakarxvanunx
BeVdisutatxde. adanenxV nAvu vacanapariBASeyalilx AcAra\-liMgada
sAkASxtAkxravenunxtetxVve. anaMtara kuMDaliniyu AdhArada meVliruva
sAvxdhiSAThxnacakarxvanunx BeVdisi alilxruva guruliMgavanUnx,
anaMtara sAvxdhi\-SAThx\-nada meVliruva maNipUrakacakarxvanunx BeVdisi,
alilxruva shivaliMgavanUnx kUDutatxde. anaMtara adu
haqdayasAthxnadalilxruva anAhatacakarxvanunx BeVdisi alilxruva
jaMgamaliMgavanUnx kUDutatxde, anaMtara kaMThasAthxnadalilxruva
vishudadhxcakarxvanunx BeVdisi alilxruva parxsAdaliMgavanunx
kUDutatxde.}}
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{taleyalilx matetxraDu cakarxgaLive. hubibxna madhayxdalilxruva
  cakarxkekx AjAcnx\-cakarxveMdu hesaru. sAdhakanu anaMtara
  kuMDaliyanunx inUnx meVlakekx taMdu AjAcnxcakarxvanunx BeVdisi,
  alilxruva mahAliMgavanunx sAkASxtakxrisikoLuLxtAtxne. koneyalilx,

  aikayxvAgutatxde. vacanapariBASeyalilx idakekx liMgAMgasAmarasayxveMdu hesaru. shAkatxra parxkAra kuMDaliniyu shivanalilx aikayxvAguvudeV paramadheyxVya; vacanakArara parxkAra, aMganu

\begin{entry}

\begin{entry}

  vayxtAyxsa\-mADi, parashivanige sugaMdhavananxSeTxV apiRsabeVku. oMdu
  vishAlAthaRdalilx, I riVti vayxtAyxsa mADade elalxdanUnx shivanige
  apiRsabeVkeMdu manasusx mADidare, apiRsidudelAlx sugaMdhavAgi
  pariNamisutatxde. aMdare nijavAda Bakatxnu sugaMdha beVku, dugaRMdha
beVDa enanxde, elalxdanUnx shiva\-nige apiRsi, anaMtara tAnu
anuBavisutAtxne. shivanige apiRsida \hbox{gaMdhada} pUvaRguNagaLu hoVgi, adu
shudadhx gaMdha (sugaMdha)vAgutatxde. adanunx avanu liMgaviruvalilxge
hoVgi, keYyiMda apiRsade, manasisxnalilxyeV liMgavanunx nenedu,
manasisxniMdaleV adanunx liMgakekx apiRsutAtxne. idanenx
cenanxbasavaNaNxnavaru `dugaRMdhava kaLedu sugaMdhavanu GArxNadiMda
liMgakakxpiRsuvalilx...' enunxtAtxre. (3:228)}}
